		- PARENT = { cfront , tokenList , tok , * , next , for , Token , simplecpp , }
		- CHILD  = { continue , }
		- PRED   = { location , == , && , previous , || , op , line , != , tok , if , }
		- SUCC   = { emptyString , file , location , line , tok , directive , Directive , }
